+package main
+
+import (
+"encoding/json"
+"fmt"
+
+"github.com/coder/coder/v2/cli/cliui"
+"github.com/coder/coder/v2/codersdk"
+)
+
+func main() {
+fmt.Println("=== Testing RichMultiSelect logic ===\n")
+
+// Test 1: Empty defaults, options present
+fmt.Println("Test 1: Empty defaults with options")
+opts1 := cliui.RichMultiSelectOptions{
+Options: []codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption{
+{Name: "Option 1", Value: "opt1", Description: "First option"},
+{Name: "Option 2", Value: "opt2", Description: "Second option"},
+{Name: "Option 3", Value: "opt3", Description: "Third option"},
+},
+Defaults: []string{},
+}
+fmt.Printf("Options count: %d\n", len(opts1.Options))
+fmt.Printf("Defaults count: %d\n", len(opts1.Defaults))
+fmt.Println("Expected behavior: All options should be available for selection, none pre-selected")
+fmt.Println()
+
+// Test 2: Non-empty defaults
+fmt.Println("Test 2: Non-empty defaults with options")
+opts2 := cliui.RichMultiSelectOptions{
+Options: []codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption{
+{Name: "Option 1", Value: "opt1", Description: "First option"},
+{Name: "Option 2", Value: "opt2", Description: "Second option"},
+{Name: "Option 3", Value: "opt3", Description: "Third option"},
+},
+Defaults: []string{"opt1", "opt3"},
+}
+fmt.Printf("Options count: %d\n", len(opts2.Options))
+fmt.Printf("Defaults count: %d\n", len(opts2.Defaults))
+fmt.Println("Expected behavior: All options available, opt1 and opt3 pre-selected")
+fmt.Println()
+
+// Test 3: Verify old buggy behavior would have failed
+fmt.Println("Test 3: Demonstrating the bug fix")
+fmt.Println("Old behavior: Would unmarshal DefaultValue as options[]")
+
+param := codersdk.TemplateVersionParameter{
+Name:         "test_param",
+Type:         "list(string)",
+FormType:     "multi-select",
+DefaultValue: "[]", // Empty default - this is what caused the bug!
+Options: []codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption{
+{Name: "Option 1", Value: "opt1", Description: "First option"},
+{Name: "Option 2", Value: "opt2", Description: "Second option"},
+{Name: "Option 3", Value: "opt3", Description: "Third option"},
+},
+}
+
+// Simulate old buggy code
+var oldBuggyOptions []string
+json.Unmarshal([]byte(param.DefaultValue), &oldBuggyOptions)
+fmt.Printf("Old buggy approach - options from DefaultValue: %v (length: %d)\n", oldBuggyOptions, len(oldBuggyOptions))
+fmt.Println("This would result in NO OPTIONS being shown!")
+fmt.Println()
+
+// New correct behavior
+fmt.Println("New correct approach:")
+fmt.Printf("Available options from param.Options: %d\n", len(param.Options))
+for _, opt := range param.Options {
+displayText := opt.Name
+if opt.Description != "" {
+displayText += ": " + opt.Description
+}
+fmt.Printf("  - %s (value: %s)\n", displayText, opt.Value)
+}
+
+var defaults []string
+json.Unmarshal([]byte(param.DefaultValue), &defaults)
+fmt.Printf("Defaults from DefaultValue: %v (length: %d)\n", defaults, len(defaults))
+
+fmt.Println("\n=== SUCCESS ===")
+fmt.Println("The fix ensures that:")
+fmt.Println("1. Options come from templateVersionParameter.Options (not DefaultValue)")
+fmt.Println("2. Defaults come from templateVersionParameter.DefaultValue")
+fmt.Println("3. Descriptions are properly displayed")
+}

+package main
+
+import (
+"encoding/json"
+"fmt"
+
+"github.com/coder/coder/v2/codersdk"
+)
+
+func main() {
+fmt.Println("Test Case 1: MultiSelect with Options but empty DefaultValue")
+param1 := codersdk.TemplateVersionParameter{
+Name:        "test_param",
+Type:        "list(string)",
+FormType:    "multi-select",
+DefaultValue: "[]", // Empty default
+Options: []codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption{
+{Name: "Option 1", Value: "opt1", Description: "First option"},
+{Name: "Option 2", Value: "opt2", Description: "Second option"},
+{Name: "Option 3", Value: "opt3", Description: "Third option"},
+},
+}
+
+// Simulate the current buggy logic from parameter.go line 37-63
+var options []string
+err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(param1.DefaultValue), &options)
+if err != nil {
+fmt.Printf("ERROR: %v\n", err)
+}
+fmt.Printf("Options extracted from DefaultValue: %v\n", options)
+fmt.Printf("Length of options: %d\n", len(options))
+fmt.Printf("Available Options in parameter: %d\n", len(param1.Options))
+for _, opt := range param1.Options {
+fmt.Printf("  - %s: %s (%s)\n", opt.Name, opt.Value, opt.Description)
+}
+
+fmt.Println("\nTest Case 2: MultiSelect with Options and non-empty DefaultValue")
+param2 := codersdk.TemplateVersionParameter{
+Name:        "test_param2",
+Type:        "list(string)",
+FormType:    "multi-select",
+DefaultValue: `["opt1", "opt2"]`, // Non-empty default
+Options: []codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption{
+{Name: "Option 1", Value: "opt1", Description: "First option"},
+{Name: "Option 2", Value: "opt2", Description: "Second option"},
+{Name: "Option 3", Value: "opt3", Description: "Third option"},
+},
+}
+
+var defaults2 []string
+err = json.Unmarshal([]byte(param2.DefaultValue), &defaults2)
+if err != nil {
+fmt.Printf("ERROR: %v\n", err)
+}
+fmt.Printf("Defaults extracted from DefaultValue: %v\n", defaults2)
+fmt.Printf("Length of defaults: %d\n", len(defaults2))
+fmt.Printf("Available Options in parameter: %d\n", len(param2.Options))
+for _, opt := range param2.Options {
+fmt.Printf("  - %s: %s (%s)\n", opt.Name, opt.Value, opt.Description)
+}
+
+fmt.Println("\n=== ISSUE IDENTIFIED ===")
+fmt.Println("The current code in parameter.go lines 42-45 unmarshals DefaultValue into 'options'")
+fmt.Println("Then lines 48-49 set MultiSelectOptions.Options = options and .Defaults = options")
+fmt.Println("This means:")
+fmt.Println("1. If DefaultValue is empty [], no options are shown (BUG 1)")
+fmt.Println("2. The parameter.Options field is completely ignored")
+fmt.Println("3. Descriptions in Options are ignored (BUG 2)")
+
+fmt.Println("\n=== CORRECT BEHAVIOR ===")
+fmt.Println("Should extract available options from param.Options (showing value)")
+availableOptions := make([]string, len(param1.Options))
+for i, opt := range param1.Options {
+availableOptions[i] = opt.Value
+}
+fmt.Printf("Available options: %v\n", availableOptions)
+
+var selectedDefaults []string
+_ = json.Unmarshal([]byte(param1.DefaultValue), &selectedDefaults)
+fmt.Printf("Default selections: %v\n", selectedDefaults)
+
+fmt.Println("\nFor display, should show Name with Description:")
+for _, opt := range param1.Options {
+displayText := opt.Name
+if opt.Description != "" {
+displayText += ": " + opt.Description
+}
+fmt.Printf("  - %s\n", displayText)
+}
+}

+package main
+
+import (
+"encoding/json"
+"fmt"
+"os"
+
+"github.com/coder/coder/v2/cli/cliui"
+"github.com/coder/coder/v2/codersdk"
+"github.com/coder/serpent"
+)
+
+func main() {
+// Test case 1: Empty defaults with options
+fmt.Println("=== Test 1: Empty defaults with options ===")
+param1 := codersdk.TemplateVersionParameter{
+Name:         "test_param1",
+Type:         "list(string)",
+FormType:     "multi-select",
+DefaultValue: "[]", // Empty default
+Options: []codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption{
+{Name: "Option 1", Value: "opt1", Description: "First option"},
+{Name: "Option 2", Value: "opt2", Description: "Second option"},
+{Name: "Option 3", Value: "opt3", Description: "Third option"},
+},
+}
+
+// Use RichParameter (which internally calls RichMultiSelect)
+cmd := &serpent.Command{
+Handler: func(inv *serpent.Invocation) error {
+result, err := cliui.RichParameter(inv, param1, nil)
+if err != nil {
+return err
+}
+fmt.Printf("Result: %s\n", result)
+
+var values []string
+if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(result), &values); err != nil {
+return err
+}
+fmt.Printf("Values: %v\n", values)
+return nil
+},
+}
+
+inv := cmd.Invoke()
+inv.Stdin = os.Stdin
+inv.Stdout = os.Stdout
+inv.Stderr = os.Stderr
+
+if err := inv.Run(); err != nil {
+fmt.Printf("Error: %v\n", err)
+}
+
+fmt.Println()
+
+// Test case 2: Non-empty defaults with options
+fmt.Println("=== Test 2: Non-empty defaults with options ===")

+},

+if err != nil {
+return err
+}

+if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(result), &values); err != nil {
+return err
+}
+fmt.Printf("Values: %v\n", values)
+return nil
+},
+}
+
+inv2 := cmd2.Invoke()
+inv2.Stdin = os.Stdin
+inv2.Stdout = os.Stdout
+inv2.Stderr = os.Stderr
+
+if err := inv2.Run(); err != nil {
+fmt.Printf("Error: %v\n", err)
+}
+
+fmt.Println()
+
+// Test case 3: Options without descriptions
+fmt.Println("=== Test 3: Options without descriptions ===")
+param3 := codersdk.TemplateVersionParameter{
+Name:         "test_param3",

+                _, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout, "  "+strings.TrimSpace(strings.Join(strings.Split(templateVersionParameter.DescriptionPlaintext, "\n"), "\n  "))+"\n")
+        }

+        defaultValue := templateVersionParameter.DefaultValue
+        if v, ok := defaultOverrides[templateVersionParameter.Name]; ok {
+                defaultValue = v
+        }
+
+        var err error
+        var value string
+        switch {
+        case templateVersionParameter.Type == "list(string)":
+                // Move the cursor up a single line for nicer display!
+                _, _ = fmt.Fprint(inv.Stdout, "\033[1A")
+
+                // Parse defaults from DefaultValue
+                var defaults []string
+                err = json.Unmarshal([]byte(templateVersionParameter.DefaultValue), &defaults)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return "", err
+                }
+
+                // If there are options defined, use RichMultiSelect to show names and descriptions
+                if len(templateVersionParameter.Options) > 0 {
+                        values, err := RichMultiSelect(inv, RichMultiSelectOptions{
+                                Options:  templateVersionParameter.Options,
+                                Defaults: defaults,
+                        })
+                        if err == nil {
+                                v, err := json.Marshal(&values)
+                                if err != nil {
+                                        return "", err
+                                }
+
+                                _, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout)
+                                pretty.Fprintf(
+                                        inv.Stdout,
+                                        DefaultStyles.Prompt, "%s\n", strings.Join(values, ", "),
+                                )
+                                value = string(v)
+                        }
+                } else {
+                        // Fallback: if no options are defined, use defaults as options
+                        values, err := MultiSelect(inv, MultiSelectOptions{
+                                Options:  defaults,
+                                Defaults: defaults,
+                        })
+                        if err == nil {
+                                v, err := json.Marshal(&values)
+                                if err != nil {
+                                        return "", err
+                                }
+
+                                _, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout)
+                                pretty.Fprintf(
+                                        inv.Stdout,
+                                        DefaultStyles.Prompt, "%s\n", strings.Join(values, ", "),
+                                )
+                                value = string(v)
+                        }
+                }
+        case len(templateVersionParameter.Options) > 0:
+                // Move the cursor up a single line for nicer display!
+                _, _ = fmt.Fprint(inv.Stdout, "\033[1A")
+                var richParameterOption *codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption
+                richParameterOption, err = RichSelect(inv, RichSelectOptions{
+                        Options:    templateVersionParameter.Options,
+                        Default:    defaultValue,
+                        HideSearch: true,
+                })
+                if err == nil {
+                        _, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout)
+                        pretty.Fprintf(inv.Stdout, DefaultStyles.Prompt, "%s\n", richParameterOption.Name)
+                        value = richParameterOption.Value
+                }
+        default:
+                text := "Enter a value"
+                if !templateVersionParameter.Required {
+                        text += fmt.Sprintf(" (default: %q)", defaultValue)
+                }
+                text += ":"
+
+                value, err = Prompt(inv, PromptOptions{
+                        Text: Bold(text),
+                        Validate: func(value string) error {
+                                return validateRichPrompt(value, templateVersionParameter)
+                        },
+                })
+                value = strings.TrimSpace(value)
+        }
+        if err != nil {
+                return "", err
+        }
+
+        // If they didn't specify anything, use the default value if set.
+        if len(templateVersionParameter.Options) == 0 && value == "" {
+                value = defaultValue
+        }
+
+        return value, nil
 }

+        m, err := p.Run()

+                return "", err
+        }
+

+        if !ok {
+                return "", xerrors.New(fmt.Sprintf("unknown model found %T (%+v)", m, m))
+        }
+
+        if model.canceled {
+                return "", ErrCanceled
+        }
+

 type MultiSelectOptions struct {
-	Message           string
-	Options           []string
-	Defaults          []string
-	EnableCustomInput bool
+        Message           string
+        Options           []string
+        Defaults          []string
+        EnableCustomInput bool
+}
+
+type RichMultiSelectOptions struct {
+        Options  []codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption
+        Defaults []string
+}
+
+// RichMultiSelect displays a list of user options including name and description for multi-selection.
+func RichMultiSelect(inv *serpent.Invocation, richOptions RichMultiSelectOptions) ([]string, error) {
+        // Similar hack is applied to Select() and MultiSelect()
+        if flag.Lookup("test.v") != nil {
+                return richOptions.Defaults, nil
+        }
+
+        opts := make([]string, len(richOptions.Options))
+        defaultOpts := make([]string, 0, len(richOptions.Defaults))
+        
+        // Create a map for quick lookup of values in defaults
+        defaultMap := make(map[string]bool)
+        for _, d := range richOptions.Defaults {
+                defaultMap[d] = true
+        }
+        
+        for i, option := range richOptions.Options {
+                line := option.Name
+                if len(option.Description) > 0 {
+                        line += ": " + option.Description
+                }
+                opts[i] = line
+                
+                // If this option's value is in the defaults, add the formatted line to defaultOpts
+                if defaultMap[option.Value] {
+                        defaultOpts = append(defaultOpts, line)
+                }
+        }
+        
+        selected, err := MultiSelect(inv, MultiSelectOptions{
+                Options:  opts,
+                Defaults: defaultOpts,
+        })
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+        
+        // Map the selected display strings back to their values
+        values := make([]string, 0, len(selected))
+        for _, sel := range selected {
+                for i, opt := range opts {
+                        if opt == sel {
+                                values = append(values, richOptions.Options[i].Value)
+                                break
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+        
+        return values, nil
 }

+        defer closeSignalHandler()

+        }

+        }
+

+                return nil, ErrCanceled

+        }

+        var value string

+                _, _ = fmt.Fprint(inv.Stdout, "\033[1A")
+

+                var defaults []string
+                err = json.Unmarshal([]byte(templateVersionParameter.DefaultValue), &defaults)
+                if err != nil {
+                        return "", err
+                }
+
+                // If there are options defined, use RichMultiSelect to show names and descriptions
+                if len(templateVersionParameter.Options) > 0 {
+                        values, err := RichMultiSelect(inv, RichMultiSelectOptions{
+                                Options:  templateVersionParameter.Options,
+                                Defaults: defaults,
+                        })

+                                v, err := json.Marshal(&values)
+                                if err != nil {
+                                        return "", err
+                                }

+                                _, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout)

+                                        inv.Stdout,
+                                        DefaultStyles.Prompt, "%s\n", strings.Join(values, ", "),
+                                )
+                                value = string(v)
+                        }
+                } else {
+                        // Fallback: if no options are defined, use defaults as options
+                        values, err := MultiSelect(inv, MultiSelectOptions{
+                                Options:  defaults,
+                                Defaults: defaults,
+                        })
+                        if err == nil {
+                                v, err := json.Marshal(&values)
+                                if err != nil {
+                                        return "", err
+                                }

+                                _, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout)
+                                pretty.Fprintf(
+                                        inv.Stdout,
+                                        DefaultStyles.Prompt, "%s\n", strings.Join(values, ", "),
+                                )
+                                value = string(v)
+                        }
+                }

+                // Move the cursor up a single line for nicer display!
+                _, _ = fmt.Fprint(inv.Stdout, "\033[1A")

+                        Options:    templateVersionParameter.Options,
+                        Default:    defaultValue,
+                        HideSearch: true,
+                })
+                if err == nil {
+                        _, _ = fmt.Fprintln(inv.Stdout)
+                        pretty.Fprintf(inv.Stdout, DefaultStyles.Prompt, "%s\n", richParameterOption.Name)
+                        value = richParameterOption.Value
+                }
+        default:
+                text := "Enter a value"
+                if !templateVersionParameter.Required {
+                        text += fmt.Sprintf(" (default: %q)", defaultValue)
+                }
+                text += ":"
+
+                value, err = Prompt(inv, PromptOptions{
+                        Text: Bold(text),
+                        Validate: func(value string) error {
+                                return validateRichPrompt(value, templateVersionParameter)
+                        },
+                })
+                value = strings.TrimSpace(value)
+        }
+        if err != nil {
+                return "", err
+        }
+
+        // If they didn't specify anything, use the default value if set.
+        if len(templateVersionParameter.Options) == 0 && value == "" {
+                value = defaultValue
+        }
+
+        return value, nil
 }

+
+type RichMultiSelectOptions struct {
+        Options  []codersdk.TemplateVersionParameterOption
+        Defaults []string
+}
+
+// RichMultiSelect displays a list of user options including name and description for multi-selection.
+func RichMultiSelect(inv *serpent.Invocation, richOptions RichMultiSelectOptions) ([]string, error) {
+        // Similar hack is applied to Select() and MultiSelect()
+        if flag.Lookup("test.v") != nil {
+                return richOptions.Defaults, nil
+        }
+
+        opts := make([]string, len(richOptions.Options))
+        defaultOpts := make([]string, 0, len(richOptions.Defaults))
+        
+        // Create a map for quick lookup of values in defaults
+        defaultMap := make(map[string]bool)
+        for _, d := range richOptions.Defaults {
+                defaultMap[d] = true
+        }
+        
+        for i, option := range richOptions.Options {
+                line := option.Name
+                if len(option.Description) > 0 {
+                        line += ": " + option.Description
+                }
+                opts[i] = line
+                
+                // If this option's value is in the defaults, add the formatted line to defaultOpts
+                if defaultMap[option.Value] {
+                        defaultOpts = append(defaultOpts, line)
+                }
+        }
+        
+        selected, err := MultiSelect(inv, MultiSelectOptions{
+                Options:  opts,
+                Defaults: defaultOpts,
+        })
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+        
+        // Map the selected display strings back to their values
+        values := make([]string, 0, len(selected))
+        for _, sel := range selected {
+                for i, opt := range opts {
+                        if opt == sel {
+                                values = append(values, richOptions.Options[i].Value)
+                                break
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+        
+        return values, nil
 }

-	if flag.Lookup("test.v") != nil {
-		return opts.Defaults, nil
-	}
-
-	options := make([]*multiSelectOption, len(opts.Options))
-	for i, option := range opts.Options {
-		chosen := false

+                        chosen: chosen,
+                }

+                tea.WithOutput(inv.Stdout),
+        )
+
+        closeSignalHandler := installSignalHandler(p)
+        defer closeSignalHandler()
+
+        m, err := p.Run()
+        if err != nil {
+                return nil, err
+        }
+
+        model, ok := m.(multiSelectModel)
+        if !ok {
+                return nil, xerrors.New(fmt.Sprintf("unknown model found %T (%+v)", m, m))
+        }
+
+        if model.canceled {
+                return nil, ErrCanceled
+        }
+
+        return model.selectedOptions(), nil

+        var cmd tea.Cmd
+
+        if m.isCustomInputMode {
+                return m.handleCustomInputMode(msg)
+        }
+
+        switch msg := msg.(type) {
+        case terminateMsg:
+                m.canceled = true
+                return m, tea.Quit
+
+        case tea.KeyMsg:
+                switch msg.Type {
+                case tea.KeyCtrlC:
+                        m.canceled = true
+                        return m, tea.Quit
+
+                case tea.KeyEnter:
+                        // Switch to custom input mode if we're on the "+ Add custom value:" option
+                        if m.enableCustomInput && m.cursor == len(m.filteredOptions()) {
+                                m.isCustomInputMode = true
+                                return m, nil
+                        }
+                        if len(m.options) != 0 {
+                                m.selected = true
+                                return m, tea.Quit
+                        }
+
+                case tea.KeySpace:
+                        options := m.filteredOptions()
+                        if len(options) != 0 {
+                                options[m.cursor].chosen = !options[m.cursor].chosen
+                        }
+                        // We back out early here otherwise a space will be inserted
+                        // into the search field.
+                        return m, nil
+
+                case tea.KeyUp:
+                        maxIndex := m.getMaxIndex()
+                        if m.cursor > 0 {
+                                m.cursor--
+                        } else {
+                                m.cursor = maxIndex
+                        }
+
+                case tea.KeyDown:
+                        maxIndex := m.getMaxIndex()
+                        if m.cursor < maxIndex {
+                                m.cursor++
+                        } else {
+                                m.cursor = 0
+                        }
+
+                case tea.KeyRight:
+                        options := m.filteredOptions()
+                        for _, option := range options {
+                                option.chosen = true
+                        }
+
+                case tea.KeyLeft:
+                        options := m.filteredOptions()
+                        for _, option := range options {
+                                option.chosen = false
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+
+        oldSearch := m.search.Value()
+        m.search, cmd = m.search.Update(msg)
+
+        // If the search query has changed then we need to ensure
+        // the cursor is still pointing at a valid option.
+        if m.search.Value() != oldSearch {
+                options := m.filteredOptions()
+                if m.cursor > len(options)-1 {
+                        m.cursor = max(0, len(options)-1)
+                }
+        }
+
+        return m, cmd
 }
